  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=7.6)
    The story successfully integrates all assigned elements into a cohesive whole that feels organic rather than forced. The juxtaposition of perfect miniatures against Elias's secret rebellion creates lingering questions about authenticity versus appearance. The prose occasionally becomes slightly overwrought but generally maintains clarity while supporting the emotional weight of the narrative.
